Ask HP Back $1249.00 $1949.00 To top Features Buy Back Features HP EliteBook 1040 HP EliteBook 1040 Everything a business Ultrabook™ 1 should be. The sophisticated style of the world's thinnest 14-inch diagonal business-class notebook2 complements its innovative performance, security, and manageability features. View options Now featuring  HP Sure View integrated privacy screen3 Carry less. Do more. Work confidently with the thin, elegant, and durable HP EliteBook 1040 with a strong all-metal diamond cut design that passed MIL-STD 810G testing4. Designed for productivity The HP EliteBook 1040 helps you stay productive and safe in and out of the office, combining power and speed with protection from malware and visual hacking. Impressive performance 6th Gen Intel® Core™ processors5, Windows 106, long battery life, up to 16GB of memory, and PCIe SSDs. Keep it private Optional HP Sure View3 integrated privacy screen. Give your fingers a break Enjoy a remarkable balance of comfort with the spill-resistant, backlit7 HP Premium Keyboard. Keep visual hackers in the dark Instantly protect against visual hacking with HP Sure View3, an optional integrated privacy screen developed by HP, featuring 3M privacy technology. Watch video Elite Premium features Processor Ultimate performance Power through your day with a 6th Gen Intel® Core™ processors, including the Intel® Core™ i7 processor.5 Ports Easy connection Essential ports provide convenient connections to peripheral devices. The HDMI port allows fast connections to monitors and projectors, while two USB 3.0 charging ports and one USB-C™ port allow for hassle free charging of mobile devices. Security Self-healing safeguard Protect, detect, and recover from malicious BIOS attacks with HP Sure Start with Dynamic Protection8 - the industry's first self-healing BIOS that monitors and corrects BIOS corruption in real-time. Reliability Field ready Never fear bumps and minor spills. The thin and light HP EliteBook 1040 endures 120,000 of HP's Total Test Process and passed MIL-STD 810G testing4. Designed for collaboration. Collaborate with colleagues from practically anywhere with optional WWAN9, a 720p webcam, HP Noise Reduction Software and Audio by Bang & Olufsen. HP Sure View integrated privacy screen is an optional feature that must be configured at purchase. MIL-STD testing is not intended to demonstrate fitness for U.S. Department of Defense contract requirements or for military use. Test results are not a guarantee of future performance under these test conditions. Damage under the MIL STD test conditions or any accidental damage requires an optional HP Accidental Damage Protection Care Pack. Multi-Core is designed to improve performance of certain software products. Not all customers or software applications will necessarily benefit from use of this technology. Performance and clock frequency will vary depending on application workload and your hardware and software configurations. Intel's numbering is not a measurement of higher performance. Not all features are available in all editions or versions of Windows. Systems may require upgraded and/or separately purchased hardware, drivers and/or software to take full advantage of Windows functionality. Windows 10 is automatically updated, which is always enabled. ISP fees may apply and additional requirements may apply over time for updates. See http://www.microsoft.com. Items sold by HP.com are not for immediate resale. Orders that do not comply with HP.com terms, conditions, and limitations may be cancelled. Contract and volume customers not eligible. HP’s MSRP is subject to discount. HP’s MSRP price is shown as either a stand-alone price or as a strike-through price with a discounted or promotional price also listed. Discounted or promotional pricing is indicated by the presence of an additional higher MSRP strike-through price. Correct prices and promotions are validated at the time your order is placed. These terms apply only to products sold by HP.com; reseller offers may vary. Items sold by HP.com are not for immediate resale. Orders that do not comply with HP.com terms, conditions, and limitations may be cancelled. Contract and volume customers not eligible.
HP’s MSRP is subject to discount. HP’s MSRP price is shown as either a stand-alone price or as a strike-through price with a discounted or promotional price also listed. Discounted or promotional pricing is indicated by the presence of an additional higher MSRP strike-through price.
The following applies to HP systems with Intel 6th Gen and other future-generation processors on systems shipping with Windows 7, Windows 8, Windows 8.1 or Windows 10 Pro systems downgraded to Windows 7 Professional, Windows 8 Pro, or Windows 8.1: This version of Windows running with the processor or chipsets used in this system has limited support from Microsoft. For more information about Microsoft’s support, please see Microsoft’s Support Lifecycle FAQ at https://support.microsoft.com/lifecycle
